name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Deluxe Double Room
info:Stayed in April 2023
info:Solo travelers
info:2 Reviews
rating:3.7
posted:Posted April 16, 2023
msg:The location of Pan Pacific hotel is excellent as it was a stone throw away to metro station. However, this hotel catered to a lot of tour groups and this hotel is very old already. The interior room design, well is old. I can see they did some mini touch up here and there. First time, i see aircon control is old-fashioned type, with a round button to turn for temperature. However, the first few nights was hot for me, as the aircon is centralised, and the internal aircon control do not work at all. Hence, you can inform the counter receptionist staff to do an adjustment in their central airon system. Hotel breakfast is quite the standard, quite a lot to choose from. However, I encountered some scams in their breakfast restaurant where some guests dressed like monks asking you to donate for some monies. Therefore, do take note on this. They try to create small conversations with you and try to predict your future, and of course ending is ask you to donate money. Not sure, why such a big hotel has such scam happening, i have been traveling for over 3 decades and this is my first time encounter of scam inside hotel. Hence, take note of this.. probably is just my luck. 

Staff are very friendly, polite and helpful. No doubt in that. The room i stayed is quite huge and overall is ok just that the bed is not comfy.

name:s‚Äçi‚Äç ‚Äçk‚Äçn‚Äçi‚Äçg‚Äçh‚Äçt
info:Deluxe Double Room
info:Stayed in January 2023
info:Couples
info:2 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted February 1, 2023
msg:Fantastic hotel with amazing staff that are not only genuinely friendly but helpful and conversant in English. 
Pro's - great location close to a metro and walking or biking distance to restaurants and bars. Wonderful breakfast with wide selection of freshly cooked food. Gym was large enough for a workout. Room facilities all worked with enough hot water at all times of the day and night. Congenial staff from front door man to the breakfast host, cleaning staff and front desk. Internet good enough. View of the river from room. Big bed and bath - perfect for couples!
Con's - room was too warm and cooling system didn't do much to cool the room - needed to open the door to get some air circulation. Spa wasn't open perhaps due to CNY. Television needs to be updated and some more cable channels added for movies when relaxing at night. Breakfast was too busy with too many people - perhaps this needs to be monitored more closely as the scramble for tables at 9.30am was very hectic. 
Advice to people considering Pan Pacific. I highly recommend this hotel as its great value for money but get down early to breakfast to beat the crowd.

I immediately asked to change rooms, and the front desk changed it to the 12th floor, facing the road. This room was okay, much better than the previous one, with a double sofa, a desk and an office chair. As for hygiene, it was good and very clean; 2. Service: The room service and cleaning ladies were very enthusiastic and responded quickly, which was very satisfactory; 3. Dining: The breakfast was very ordinary, the taste was average, and there were not many dishes. However, the dinner on the 3rd floor was good, the price was reasonable, and the quantity was sufficient. In particular, a voucher was given when I checked in, which was cheaper than eating at a small restaurant outside. Attached are pictures of the ginger duck set meal and shacha noodles, which were delicious and cheap; 4. Location: The location of the hotel is average, there are no places to visit nearby. There are a few snack shops, but I haven't tried them. The biggest advantage is that it is close to the subway. Just walk about 100 or 200 meters and you will reach Exit 1A of Jianye Road Station on Line 2 (it is recommended to take Exit 1B, which is dozens of meters away and has an elevator, while Exit 1A does not). It is also not far from the ferry terminal, about 20 minutes' walk.

msg:For families with young children, the pros and cons of this hotel are obvious. But if I have another chance, I think I will still choose Pan Pacific without hesitation.
Let me talk about the disadvantages first: the entire building is a tower structure with limited internal space, so compared to the 60-70 square meter twin room we stayed in a few days ago, the area of each room in this hotel is not large. In addition, for parent-child travel, the hotel only has an outdoor swimming pool, no indoor swimming pool and parent-child playground, and there are not enough recreational facilities.
Besides the advantages, the service and software are very good. We booked a twin room, but it was too uncomfortable to squeeze a 1.2 bed with an adult when the child grew up, so we contacted the front desk to make a shared bed, and we got a quick response and arranged it properly. The family of three slept It was super comfortable. In addition, this is the first hotel I have stayed in that offers mouthwash, and the structure of the bathtub and shower is very convenient. After soaking in the bathtub, the child can be taken out to rinse directly. The details of the hotel brand in Singapore can be seen Very particular about quality. In addition, I would like to praise the service staff Ye Meilan in terms of room cleaning.
